< Review>
There is a real live person there for assistance!

This Amazon Prime location is an alternative to the lockers you see at 7-11s where you can pick up items purchased online.

Plenty of parking, it's right off of the Pacific Highway near the Old Town Transit Center, Marine Corps Recruit Depot and what used to be known as SPAWAR.

When purchasing an item online or through the Amazon app, if this location is convenient for you then it's better than a locker where there is no Amazon personnel to answer your questions.</Review>

Its the place to be if craving for homemade like Gujarati style Indian food. Curries/daal and food in general will be on sweeter side as it should be traditionally. Tried their mini and gujarati thali and they were good. I ordered from them on back to back days and got same curries/daal both days hence i cannot comment on the freshness of the food with the exception of Rotis/Poori which are freshly made for your thali. Quantity was less for the price. For takeaway, they use styrofoam containers which is non-recyclable; hope they upgrade to better environment friendly options. I recommend Rajdhani restaurant in Artesia for unlimited Thali and ultimate fresh food without having to burn your pockets.<//text>

<username>Scotty Sanderson</username><date>1626807488370<//date><Rate>5< /Rate><Text>Exceptional Technicians with Fantastic Service and Quality Products!!

With a 27 year old AC unit and a 43 year old gas unit in our HVAC system, we were due for a change.  We wanted to check on a whole house fan as well and insullation.

We selected Right Now Air & Solar because they have had a long very positive  record of excellent service, and they installed the  HVAC system where my wife works.

Adam came out to talk with us about their HVAC systems, a whole house fan, and also insulation, He is knowledgeable, down-to-earth, personable, and very helpful!  We had planned to have the work done based on what we could afford early next year.  With PG&E rebates and other breaks, the price was so affordable that we said do it NOW!  We were so excited to not have to wait for months and months because of their reasonable prices! Ken who is one of the supervisors came out to survey the job the same day.  He made some very helpful suggestions that were of great help.

Two days later they sent two crews out who accomplished all the work except the insullation in less than one day!  (A separate group does the insullation.)  These members of a very highly professional team of technicians do exceptioanal work!  Ricky, the Team Leader, installed the gas furnace perfectly.  He directed his teams in various duties:  Andrew and Jose worked on the ducts, sealing them to prevent outside air from coming through the system. They cleaned and vacuumed the ducts to remove dust and dirt form the system.  Miguel  and Andrew suggested the best position for the whole house fan intake in our hallway, centrally located in our home.  By the way, the whole house fan is very quiet because the fan is up in the attic, and the intake is located on a ceiling. It comes with a wireless switch to opearate it.  Chaz and Leland installed the large AC unit outside and removed the old one with great attention to all the connections and assembly required.

Each one of these crews did extra, helped each other, and was very conscientous.  Several did multiple tasks.  They had to remove a metal container formng the intake air pathway for the system under a box-like structure on which the heating unit and the fan unit sits in the garage.  They had to enlarge the intake air vent leading to the house while making a larger airtight area below the fan unit from which to draw air.  This was a challenging task which they executed flawlessly with great attention to detail and much precision.  It lowered intake noise, made the unit more efficient, and increased the airflow with less stress on the fan.  Jose and Miguel put an additional support under that box-like structure within the intake chamber to support the structure which holds and supports the heatintg and fan units. <date>1577027202325< /date><Text>I have a new German Shepherd puppy that was in serious need of basic training because of his extremely high energy. I live alone which made the desire to have him under control even more of a necessity. When he was too young to get a rabies shot (14 weeks old) I found a private trainer that would accept him for 3 week basic obedience and keep him separate from any other dogs (full shots are a necessary requirement). That did help some and gave him a decent head start, but the results after a lot of $$ and 3 weeks away from my new puppy were not everything that is advertised, which is generally the same for most puppy ‚Äúboot camps‚Äù. When he was a couple months older with all of his shots and much more work with him on my own at home, I decided to look for a more comprehensive training facility and was recommended K-9 Companions from somebody at the doggie day care he goes to. When I took him in for evaluation I anticipated that he would be going to the intermediate/off leash, 2nd level program. He was way ahead of the game from a first timer but not up to the standards K-9 Companions expects after their 1st level of obedience. He had to brush up and advance his basic training (sit, stay, heel, down, come, no, off...) for one week and was able to move on to the next level for the next 2 weeks. He came back a different dog! Still as sweet and playful as he had been from day 1, but he obeyed everything he was taught as if he was having fun doing it. When I take him for walks or anyone comes to the house, every single person who meets him can‚Äôt believe how well behaved he is for such an energetic puppy. I have even recommended to several people that they take their misbehaving or untrained adult dogs to K-9 Companions for at least basic obedience. I am certain that it has done as much for my dog‚Äôs quality of life as it has for my own enjoyment of him, and believe that would be true for any dog owner/parent. After a couple more months at home with me, he does SO well and enjoys working on everything he has learned so much, I decided to put him through more advanced training. I had already taken him back for short boarding and brush up training and he absolutely loves the staff, as they do him. No separation anxiety at all (I may have a little:) and he was genuinely excited to be back. There was no hesitation at all as the quality of the facility and the care he is given there is top notch. In researching dog training facilities the first thing reviewers and experts say is to do your homework on the facility, they are not all equal. I am 100% comfortable knowing my baby is in great hands at K-9 companions. He is currently there as I‚Äôm writing, going through his off-leash and advanced training. I could not recommend this facility and their staff any more than saying my dog is now on his third stay there and I know he is loving it as much as I will be when he comes home. The follow up training that is included has been invaluable more in the sense of training ME than my dog. He knows exactly what to do, it‚Äôs up to me to know how to properly communicate with positive reinforcement. This training is worth every penny and will pay back dividends with years of enjoyment for both you and your dog. I have owned many dogs throughout my life and never had one formally trained. I thought they were so smart (they were) but had never realized their full potential. I thought my own training that only came from years of repetition was enough. [This review is edited. I have since used their services and have added to this review! See the bottom.]

I used their service for my Great Pyrenees which is known to be a stubborn breed as it pertains to training. Upon his return he was completely leash trained, would stop at all doors and gates to be let in or out by me, but definitely the best thing was his manners. He would seem to want to understand what I wanted him to do and when he did it made him noticeably more happy.

I'm giving this place a 10/10! My only small gripe is the price but I am a firm believer in getting what you pay for.

Laura Gwin</username>
<Date>1457396868030<//Date><rating>5< /rating>< text>
I think it is important for anyone considering a free consultation at K-9 Companions to understand that the reason for the consultation is to evaluate the dogs temperament and the needs of both the dog and the client. Some dogs need to see a veterinarian for medical or temperament issues due to medical issues prior to training. Some people wish to train their dogs in a manner that is as inexpensive as possible and therefore need to spend more time being involved in the training themselves (such as driving to the facility weekly) and not boarding the dog while training. Other clients prefer to have as much as possible done for them and would prefer to board the dog (costs more) and have as much of the training as possible done for them. Some dogs actually need this level of training due to a lack of socialization or due to them being fearful or aggressive. There is no way that a trainer can tell an owner over the phone what the dog is going to need. This is why the consultation is FREE. The training prescribed could be as little as a (local) in home lesson for $100.00. It could be lessons at the facility for $250-$495. The client might want lessons done in their home (at a higher cost) or they might want the Mercedes of dog training which involves the dog staying (boarding) at the facility, followed by lesson/s in their home and a number of follow up lessons over the next year at the facility.< /text>

<Text>My family and I were in the process of moving into a new home in Lake Arrowhead and decided that our 10 month old Chesapeak Bay Retriever, Hank, needed formal training. We met with Dianne for our consultation and she assured me when Hank was done with boot camp that he would be an extremely well behaved young pup.We dropped Hank off August 2 and would be picking him up on August 23rd.

9 days into doggy training (August 11th), I received 4 back to back phone calls from a blocked number. I had my wife call and K9 Companions said Hank wasn't looking well so they took him to the vet. About an hour after they brought him back from the vet, they called saying we needed to pick him up immediately and take him to our vet. When we picked Hank up, he couldn't stand up and could barely lift his head. I had to carry him. You could tell he was extremely ill.

I took him to our local vet and the Dr took one look at Hank and said this is extremely concerning. He did X-rays and ran a parvo test. Hank came back negative for parvo and didn't have any foreign bodies lodged in his stomach but he had fluid in his lungs and was running a high fever. The vet told me, if I do not take Hank to the 24/7 emergency vet in Ontario, that Hank would not make it through the night.

I rushed Hank down the mountain and he was admitted immediately on the spot. The vet told me that Hank was in extremely rough shape and there is a chance he will not see the following morning.

Hank spent 5 days at the emergency vet with 24/7 care. Fortunately, he pulled through. He contracted a viral infection, a bacterial infection, para influenza and developed and pneumonia. Our total medical bills were over $6,000. The vet said he contracted it from this place.

K9 Companion assured us that they have never seen a case like this and that there have been no other cases of dogs getting this sick. The K9 companion staff seemed to be concerned about Hank the entire time, until it was time to talk about the bill. Dianne, the manager, was extremely worried about Hank and genuinely cared about Hanks health. She presented all the findings and bills to the owner. The owner, Laura said, there will be no reimbursement for Hanks medical bills.

K9 Companions is responsible for almost killing my dog and burying me in a financial hole. My wife stays at home with our 16 month old son. I am the sole provider. I am an Operation Enduring Freedom Veteran and still serve in the military. Our bills are worth two months of pay and we still have to take Hank in to be checked frequently to make sure his lungs have 100% recovered.

Once Hank returned home we had multiple vet visits and required attention at all times from my wife. We had to cancel a family vacation that was planned due to this nightmare. After 4 weeks of being on 3 different types of medication, having to doing breathing treatments, under constant supervision and having to be extremely careful with him, our puppy is starting to act like himself again. We are so thankful for the 24 hour Vet that saved our dogs life.

Bottom line is, do not take your dog here unless you want to deal with what we have dealt with. Morality has taken a back seat to these people and all they care about are pure profits.

***I have been in contact with another dog owner that had a similar experience as us. If you have had something similar to this, please get into contact with us!***</Text></record>

< Review>
Great historical building with interesting architectural details. Fun place to walk around or sit and watch the bay. Not too big for the less mobile people, but contains a decent variety of food stalls and shops in addition to the actual ferry ports. The farmers markets are a fun place to meet and have coffee as the morning weather on the Embarcadero is generally exquisite most of the year. Besides the fresh produce there are multiple vendors offering prepared foods. One of the unique experiences to see in San Francisco on Saturday mornings 8a-2p (also Tu/Th 10-2) and relatively easy by public transit. One of those places where locals and tourists mix.<//Review>

<user_id>116556357736267274624</user_id><username>Anton Vakulchyk</username>< time>
1535780198835<//time>
<rate>5<//rate><Text>Attention all foodies: this delectable attraction needs to be at the top of your San Francisco to-do list. The Ferry Building Marketplace is a public food market that features a variety of food stalls that act as small restaurants, snack stops and grocery stores. Here you can find everything from staples, such as seafood, burgers, Mexican food and plenty of coffee, to a Japanese delicatessen, empanada stand, nut shop and a cheese and dairy bar.

Many travelers who stopped by the Ferry Building Marketplace visited multiple times during their San Francisco trip. Visitors were impressed with the amount, variety and overall quality of eats available on-site. Though there are formal restaurants available, some visitors say the best strategy is to pick up a to-go meal and enjoy it along the scenic waterfront. And if you're not one for lines, don't come on the weekends.

You can reach the marketplace via the Embarcadero BART/Muni Station and several public buses lines. Parking is also available near the marketplace. The marketplace is open daily from 10 a.m. to 7 p.m with slightly different hours on the weekends. Restaurants and stores, however, maintain varied hours. The farmers market welcomes shoppers from 10 a.m. to 2 p.m. Tuesdays and Thursdays and from 8 a.m. to 2 p.m. on Saturdays.</Text><pictures>None< /pictures><Resp>None</Resp><Gmap_id>0x808580668d266fe7:0x229df5ca5626e6aa<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
